}

### Monarchism ###
	shared_focus = {
		id = JER_state_of_aquileia
		icon = GFX_goal_JER_state_of_aquileia
		mutually_exclusive = { focus = JER_fight_for_freedom }
		x = 4
		y = 0
		cost = 4.40
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
		allow_branch = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = obsolete_focus_branches_visibility
						option = HIDE
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = JER_fight_for_freedom
				}
			}
		}
		select_effect = {
		    hidden_effect = {
			    set_global_flag = JER_monarchist_aquileia
			    country_event = { 
				    id = aquileia.125 
					days = 7 
				}
		    }
	    }
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus JER_state_of_aquileia"
			add_political_power = 50
			custom_effect_tooltip = JER_revolution_tp
			hidden_effect = { #collapse focus tree
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = aquileian_focus
					keep_completed = yes
				}
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
			    if = {
			        limit = { has_character = JER_leonard_rodier }
			        JER_leonard_rodier = {
						remove_unit_leader_role = yes
					}
		        }
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
	}
	
	shared_focus = {
		id = JER_help_rila
		icon = GFX_goal_JER_help_rila
		prerequisite = { focus = JER_state_of_aquileia }
		bypass = {
		    OR = {
		        has_global_flag = JER_revolution_begun
				has_global_flag = JER_revolution_ended
			}
		}
		x = -2
		y = 1
		relative_position_id = JER_state_of_aquileia
		cost = 7.20
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 20
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus JER_help_rila"
			custom_effect_tooltip = JER_help_rila_tp
			add_political_power = 60
			add_war_support = 0.025
			add_to_array = { JER_revolution_countries = JEB }
			set_variable = { JERrev_selected_country = JEB }
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }
	}

		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus JER_arrest_officers"
			custom_effect_tooltip = JER_increase_support_2
			if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_idea = civilian_economy
				}
				swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = civilian_economy
					add_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
				}
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = {
				    has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
				}
				swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
					add_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
				}
			}
			else = {
			    one_random_arms_factory = yes
			}
			add_manpower = -2500
			JEB = { 
				country_event = { 
					id = aquileia.2
				} 
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER }
	}

					add_idea = limited_conscription
				}
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = { has_idea = limited_conscription }
				swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = limited_conscription
					add_idea = extensive_conscription
				}
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = { has_idea = extensive_conscription }
				swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = extensive_conscription
					add_idea = service_by_requirement
				}
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = { has_idea = service_by_requirement }
				swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = service_by_requirement
					add_idea = all_adults_serve
				}
			}
			else_if = {
			    limit = { has_idea = all_adults_serve }
				swap_ideas = {
				    remove_idea = all_adults_serve
					add_idea = scraping_the_barrel
				}
			}
		}
		search_filters = { FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS }
	}
